**Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 3:
`A*c0/(c1+c2*exp(c3*t)) + A*c4*exp(c3*t)/(c1+c2*exp(c3*t)) + A^c5*c6/(c1+c2*exp(c3*t)) + A^c5*c7*exp(c3*t)/(c1+c2*exp(c3*t)) + c8*t/(c1+c2*exp(c3*t))`

All terms have denominator (c1+c2*exp(c3*t)). Let me set c1=1, c2=0 to simplify: then denominator=1, giving A*c0 + A*c4*0 + A^c5*c6 + 0 + c8*t. This gives A*c0 + A^c5*c6 + c8*t. Set c0=0, c8=0: A^c5*c6. Missing A*exp(ct) term. 

Alternatively, let c2≠0. The terms combine to: [A*(c0+c4*exp(c3*t)) + A^c5*(c6+c7*exp(c3*t)) + c8*t] / (c1+c2*exp(c3*t)).

For GT = c_a*A^(1/3) + c_b*A*exp(c_d*t), I need to check if this rational structure in exp(c3*t) can produce it. Setting c8=0 and c5=1/3:

[A*(c0+c4*e^(c3t)) + A^(1/3)*(c6+c7*e^(c3t))] / (c1+c2*e^(c3t))

For this to equal α*A^(1/3) + β*A*e^(c3t), I need:
- A^(1/3) coefficient: (c6+c7*e^(c3t))/(c1+c2*e^(c3t)) = α (constant)
  → c7/c2 = c6/c1 = α, so c7=α*c2, c6=α*c1
- A coefficient: (c0+c4*e^(c3t))/(c1+c2*e^(c3t)) = β*e^(c3t)
  → c0+c4*e^(c3t) = β*c1*e^(c3t) + β*c2*e^(2c3t)
  
This requires β*c2=0 and c0=0, c4=β*c1. Then A coefficient = c4*e^(c3t)/c1 = β*e^(c3t). ✓ With c2=0, c1=1.

But if c2=0, the denominator is just c1, and we're back to: A*(c0+c4*e^(c3t)) + A^(1/3)*(c6+c7*e^(c3t)). Set c0=0, c7=0: A*c4*e^(c3t) + A^(1/3)*c6. With c3 negative, this matches GT! ✓

**Candidate 3 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 4:
`A²*c0/(A+c1)² + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5*exp(A*c6) + c7 + c8*t`

Has exp(A*c6) - setting c5=0 removes it. A²*c0/(A+c1)² with c0=0 removes it. Then A*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + c7 + c8*t. Set c2=0, c7=0, c8=0: A*c3*exp(c4*t). Missing A^(1/3).
**Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 5:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^c2*c3 + c4*exp(c5/(c6+t)) + c7`

Set c4=0, c7=0: A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^c2*c3. With c2=1/3, this is exactly the GT form! ✓
**Candidate 5 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 6:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*exp(c3/(c4+t)) + c5 + c6*log(A*c7+1)`

Set c2=0, c5=0: A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c6*log(A*c7+1). log(A*c7+1) ≠ A^(1/3) for all A≥0.
**Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 7:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + A*c3*log(A*c4+1) + c5 + c6*t^(1/3)`

No A^(1/3) term. A*log(A*c4+1) ≠ A^(1/3).
**Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 8:
`A²*c0/(A+c1)² + A*c2 + c3*exp(c4/(c5+t)) + c6*exp(A^c7*c8)*exp(c9*t)`

Set c0=0, c3=0: A*c2 + c6*exp(A^c7*c8)*exp(c9*t). The exp(A^c7*c8) term is exponential in A, not A^(1/3). Can't match.
**Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 9:
`A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2 + c3*log(c4*t+1) + c5*(c6*t+1)^(1/4) + c7*exp(A*c8)*log(c9*t+1)`

No A^(1/3). exp(A*c8) can't become A^(1/3).
**Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 10:
`A^(1/4)*c0*log(c1*t+1) + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*t + c6*exp(A^c7*c8)`

A^(1/4)*log(c1*t+1) ≠ A^(1/3). No A^(1/3) term available.
**Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 11:
`A²*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*exp(c6/(c7+t))`

Set c0=0, c1=0, c5=0: A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t). This is A^c2 * exp(c4*t), but GT has A*exp(ct) + A^(1/3) — two separate terms. This candidate only has one term with A dependence after zeroing. Can't match.

Wait, let me reconsider. Keep c1≠0: A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t). Set c0=0, c5=0. This gives A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t). But GT has A*exp(ct) and A^(1/3). Here A*c1 is just linear in A (no t-dependence), while A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) mixes A^c2 with exp. For GT, I need A^1*exp and A^(1/3)*constant. So set c2=1: A*c1 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) = A*(c1+c3*exp(c4*t)). Missing A^(1/3). Set c2=1/3: A^(1/3)*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c1. But A^(1/3)*exp(c4*t) ≠ A^(1/3)*constant unless c4=0, but then A*c1 has no exp decay. If c4=0: A*c1 + A^(1/3)*c3. Missing exp(ct)*A term.
**Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 12:
All terms have denominator (A+c2). Combining: [A²*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*A^c3*c4 + A*c5 + A*c6 + A*c7*exp(c1*t) + A^c3*c8 + c9] / (A+c2)

Set c3=1/3. Numerator: A²*c0*exp(c1t) + A^(4/3)*c4 + A*(c5+c6) + A*c7*exp(c1t) + A^(1/3)*c8 + c9

For this to equal (A+c2)*(α*A^(1/3) + β*A*exp(c1t)):
= α*A^(4/3) + α*c2*A^(1/3) + β*A²*exp(c1t) + β*c2*A*exp(c1t)

Matching: c0=β, c4=α, c5+c6=0, c7=β*c2, c8=α*c2, c9=0. This works! ✓
**Candidate 12 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 13:
[A²*c0*exp(c1t) + A*(c3+c4) + A*c5*exp(c1t) + c9]/(A+c2) + A^c6*c7*exp(c8*t)

For GT: need A^(1/3) and A*exp(ct). Set c6=1/3, c8=0: A^(1/3)*c7 + [A²*c0*exp(c1t) + A*(c3+c4) + A*c5*exp(c1t) + c9]/(A+c2).

Set c0=0, c3+c4=0, c9=0: A*c5*exp(c1t)/(A+c2). For this to equal β*A*exp(c1t), need c2=0, c5=β. Then total: A^(1/3)*c7 + β*A*exp(c1t). ✓
**Candidate 13 verdict: [MATCH]**
